info:Hyatt Regency Twin Room

info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:4.8
posted:Posted April 17, 2024
msg:A weekend staycation must embrace Jiading Hyatt:
/ Table lamps, chandeliers, wall lamps, different but unified in style
/ There are basins in the bathroom and toilet, and the standard room also has double basins, which is great
/ Four-petal flower patterns run through the entire room, carpets, paintings, entrance partitions, sliding door handles, elevator buttons, elevator floor tiles, and so on
/ The TV is very large, estimated to be 50 inches
/ The wall at the round table is also equipped with an HDMI socket to connect directly to the TV. My husband plugged in the PS5 and it was like being at home, COD was fine
/ The sunshade goes straight up and down, and the side is embedded in the track, so there is no light leakage on the four sides, which is the favorite of people who are afraid of light when sleeping
/ The swimming pool is 25 meters long, with no deep water area, which is definitely enough for general swimming. My husband said that there is also a pulsator washing machine with dehydration in the men's locker room, which is very convenient for drying swimming trunks. Unfortunately, our women's locker room does not have it. By the way, the opening hours are from 9 am to 9 pm

600r a night is cost-effective, isn't it?
Love it, I'll come again next time!

msg:The hotel is next to Yuanxiang Lake in Jiading New District, with Poly Theater and Jiading Library nearby, and not far from Jiading Baolong Square. However, there are not many businesses in the surrounding area, except for some catering facilities, there is nothing else to visit. The scenery of Yuanxiang Lake is good, and the appearance of the hotel is also very unique.
    The hotel has an underground garage. You must scan the code with negative nucleic acid within 48 hours to enter the elevator. The lobby is on the highest 42nd floor. The lobby is medium in size and simple in decoration. The reception is very friendly and the check-in is also fast. The floor of the accommodation goes from the lobby bar through the coffee shop to the elevator at the back. You need to swipe your card. Although the privacy and security are better, it is not very convenient to enter and exit.
    The room I stayed in was on the 40th floor. The entrance was made as a porch. The left side was the washstand, bathtub and shower room, and the right side was the toilet. The bathroom was also equipped with a small washbasin. The sanitary ware and bathroom faucets were all Kohler brands. The quality of the shower gel and soap is ok. There were no small items such as cotton swabs and sewing kits on the first day, and some were put during cleaning the next day. Supplies such as toothbrushes, combs, and disposable razors are not provided voluntarily. Hand towels, towels, and bath towels are relatively white and fluffy, but there is a burr on the first day. Only one bathrobe is provided. There is an open wardrobe in the middle of the aisle. Clothes racks, safes, slippers, flashlights, electric irons, ironing boards, etc. are all equipped.
    The room is big and the two single beds are quite big. The quilt cover, sheets and pillowcases are all clean and white. The mattress is soft and the waist support is average. The pillows are relatively fluffy. The socket switch at the bedside is more convenient to set, there are more lights in each area of the room, there are sofas, tables and chairs by the window, there are sockets set up with the functions of a dining table and a writing desk, and the floor-to-ceiling windows offer a great view of the city. The TV is quite large and has several satellite channels. There are small refrigerators, cups and tea sets, coffee tea bags, kettles, etc. in the cabinets and drawers on the side. There are more desks in the room, which is very convenient.
    The accommodation package purchased includes a light buffet dinner, with 7 dishes, 1 rice, several types of bread, several types of fruits, two types of cakes, beer drinks, and one or two dishes will be changed. On the first day, all dishes tasted average. The standard of the restaurant. The food and taste improved the next day. The variety of breakfast is very rich, the combination of Chinese and Western, the taste is more delicious, the cake and bread are more delicious. The waiter took the plate quickly too. There is no change in the dishes for two days.
    The swimming pool and gym are on the 5th floor from the elevator in the lobby, and the Chinese restaurant is also on that floor. The gym has a lot of equipment for all kinds of exercise, which is very clean and easy to use. The swimming pool is not big and shallow and suitable for children. In the afternoon, the water is not very clean. It is necessary to open the door at 9:00 in the morning to clean it up.
    All hotel staff are very polite and greet each other proactively. The surrounding environment is very good, especially the lobby or restaurant has a panoramic view. The rooms are clean, clean and very comfortable. The catering needs to be improved, especially the Chinese steamed spots.
